CEnum PeakMonitor
{
	none
	peak_analog
	peak_surround
	peak_digital
	rms_analog
	rms_surround
	rms_digital
}

CPeakMonitorTemplate PeakMonitorTemplate
{
	GraphMode (PeakMonitor none)
	GraphAlpha (0.75)
	SampleFrequency (30.0)
	PositionX (34.0)
	PositionY (288.0)
	GraphHeight (64.0)
}

//	*player (based on super)
//	taunts
//	does standing slow attacks

//	*easy
//	doesn't taunt often
//

CCharacterAICombatTemplate CharacterAICombatTemplate_Easy
{
	ProbabilityStandSlow (0.4)		// Attack:	0%	of	S1
	ProbabilityStandFast (0.2)		// Same as prob fast attck
	ProbabilityMediumAttack (0.8)	// Combo:	60%	of	M3/M4
	ProbabilityFastAttack (0.2)		// Combo:	20%	of	F2/F3/F4
	ProbabilitySlowAttack (0.2)		// Combo:	20%	of	S3/S4
	ProbabilityTripAttack (0.1)		// Combo:	20%	of	T3/T4
	ProbabilityWideAttack (0.07)		// Combo:	10%	of	W3/W4
	ProbabilityEndString (0.95)		// End Combo: 60% chance
	ProbFastCounter (0.4)			// Attack:	40%/60%	of	F/M 

	ProbStartsAttack (0.03)			// Attack:	Av 4 sec delay before attack
	TimeForCounter (7)				// 
	TimeForRecoverAttack (12)		// Recovery Counter: 0% of M1, M2 counter

	ProbMedAttackCounter (0.1)		// Counter: 50% of M, 0% of M3, 0% of M4
	MinMedAttackCountDelay (20)		//
	MaxMedAttackCountDelay (40)		//

	ProbFastAttackCounter (0.5)		// Counter: 50% of F, 0% of F3, 0% of F4
	MinFastAttackCountDelay (10)	//
	MaxFastAttackCountDelay (40)	//

	ProbSlowAttackCounter (0.5)		// Counter: 50% of S1, 0% of S3, 0% of S4
	MinSlowAttackCountDelay (20)	//
	MaxSlowAttackCountDelay (50)	//

	ProbGrabAttackCounter (0.50)	// Counter: 50% of T1, 0% of T3, 0% of T4
	MinGrabAttackCountDelay (6)		//
	MaxGrabAttackCountDelay (6)		//

	ProbTauntCounter (1.0)			// Counter: 100% of Taunt
	MinTauntCountDelay (10)			//
	MaxTauntCountDelay (30)			//

	ProbAttackRecCounter (0.25)		// Counter: 25% of Recovery
	MinAttackRecCountDelay (6)		//
	MaxAttackRecCountDelay (6)		//

	ProbTauntWhileAttack (0.3)		// Taunt: 20% Chance
	TimeBetweenBlockChange (2.0)
	TimeBetweenBlockChangeVar (0.5)
	ProbabilityBlock (0.04)
}

CCharacterAICombatTemplate CharacterAICombatTemplate_EasyW
{
	ProbabilityStandSlow (0.2)		// Attack:	0%	of	S1
	ProbabilityStandFast (0.2)		// Same as prob fast attck
	ProbabilityMediumAttack (0.8)	// Combo:	60%	of	M3/M4
	ProbabilityFastAttack (0.2)		// Combo:	20%	of	F2/F3/F4
	ProbabilitySlowAttack (0.2)		// Combo:	20%	of	S3/S4
	ProbabilityTripAttack (0.1)		// Combo:	20%	of	T3/T4
	ProbabilityWideAttack (0.07)		// Combo:	10%	of	W3/W4
	ProbabilityEndString (0.95)		// End Combo: 60% chance
	ProbFastCounter (0.4)			// Attack:	40%/60%	of	F/M 

	ProbStartsAttack (0.05)			// Attack:	Av 4 sec delay before attack
	TimeForCounter (7)				// 
	TimeForRecoverAttack (12)		// Recovery Counter: 0% of M1, M2 counter

	ProbMedAttackCounter (0.1)		// Counter: 50% of M, 0% of M3, 0% of M4

//	*blind
//	
//	Only does 3-hit combos
//	Never initiates an attack
//	Always counters during an attack never after
//	Weak against interrupt strings and trip strings
//	Never performs an unblockable attack
//  slow is useless against him
//  only c4 trip can be used against him
//  gets up slowly
//	

//	*easy
//	
//	interrupts predictably
//	always beaten by MMF combos
//	never KO's
//	

CCharacterAICombatTemplate BlindAICombatTemplate_Easy
{
	ProbabilityStandSlow (0.0)		// Attack:	20%	of	S1
	ProbabilityStandFast (0.0)		// Same as prob fast attck
	ProbabilityMediumAttack (0.0)	// Combo:	0%	of	M3/M4
	ProbabilityFastAttack (0.0)		// Combo:	0%	of	F2/F3/F4
	ProbabilitySlowAttack (0.0)		// Combo:	0%	of	S3/S4
	ProbabilityTripAttack (0)		// Combo:	0%	of	T3/T4
	ProbabilityWideAttack (0.0)		// Combo:	0%	of	W3/W4
	ProbabilityEndString (0.0)
	ProbFastCounter (1.0)			// Attack:	100%/0%	of	F/M 

	ProbStartsAttack (0.0)			// Attack:	Av 2 sec delay before attack
	TimeForCounter (7)				// 
	TimeForRecoverAttack (12)		// Recovery Counter: 0% of M1, M2 counter

	ProbMedAttackCounter (1.0)		// Counter: 100% of M, 25% of M3, 25% of M4
	MinMedAttackCountDelay (35)		//
	MaxMedAttackCountDelay (35)		//

	ProbFastAttackCounter (1.0)		// Counter: 100% of F, <25% of F3, <25% of F4
	MinFastAttackCountDelay (30)	//
	MaxFastAttackCountDelay (60)	//

	ProbSlowAttackCounter (1.0)		// Counter: 100% of S1, 100% of S3, 100% of S4

{
	ProbabilityStandSlow (0.0)		// Attack:	0%	of	S1
	ProbabilityStandFast (0.0)		// Same as prob fast attck
	ProbabilityMediumAttack (0.4)	// Combo:	60%	of	M3/M4
	ProbabilityFastAttack (0.2)		// Combo:	60%	of	F2/F3/F4
	ProbabilitySlowAttack (0.3)		// Combo:	20%	of	S3/S4
	ProbabilityTripAttack (0.1)		// Combo:	20%	of	T3/T4
	ProbabilityWideAttack (0.1)		// Combo:	10%	of	W3/W4
	ProbabilityEndString (0.97)		// End Combo: 25% chance
	ProbFastCounter (0.4)			// Attack:	40%/60%	of	F/M 

	ProbStartsAttack (0.1)			// Attack:	Av 0.4 sec delay before attack
	TimeForCounter (7)				// 
	TimeForRecoverAttack (12)		// Recovery Counter: 0% of M1, M2 counter

	ProbMedAttackCounter (0.1)		// Counter: 50% of M, 0% of M3, 0% of M4
	MinMedAttackCountDelay (20)		//
	MaxMedAttackCountDelay (40)		//

	ProbFastAttackCounter (0.5)		// Counter: 50% of F, 0% of F3, 0% of F4
	MinFastAttackCountDelay (10)	//
	MaxFastAttackCountDelay (40)	//

	ProbSlowAttackCounter (0.5)		// Counter: 50% of S1, 0% of S3, 0% of S4
	MinSlowAttackCountDelay (20)	//
	MaxSlowAttackCountDelay (50)	//

	ProbGrabAttackCounter (0.50)	// Counter: 50% of T1, 0% of T3, 0% of T4
	MinGrabAttackCountDelay (6)		//
	MaxGrabAttackCountDelay (15)	//

	ProbTauntCounter (1.0)			// Counter: 100% of Taunt
	MinTauntCountDelay (10)			//
	MaxTauntCountDelay (30)			//

	ProbAttackRecCounter (0.25)		// Counter: 25% of Recovery
	MinAttackRecCountDelay (6)		//
	MaxAttackRecCountDelay (6)		//

	ProbabilityBlock (1.0)
